  <!-- ── INTERACTIVE SCRIPTS ── -->
  <script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {

      // 1. Magnetic Buttons
      const magnets = document.querySelectorAll('.magnetic');
      magnets.forEach(magnet => {
        magnet.addEventListener('mousemove', function (e) {
          const rect = this.getBoundingClientRect();
          const x = e.clientX - rect.left - rect.width / 2;
          const y = e.clientY - rect.top - rect.height / 2;
          const strength = this.getAttribute('data-strength') || 20;
          this.style.transform = `translate(${(x / rect.width) * strength}px, ${(y / rect.height) * strength}px) scale(1.05) rotate(${(x / rect.width) * strength * 0.1}deg)`;
        });
        magnet.addEventListener('mouseleave', function () { this.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px) scale(1) rotate(0deg)'; });
      });

      // 2. Parallax Effects
      let mouseX = window.innerWidth / 2; let mouseY = window.innerHeight / 2;
      let pTargetX = 0; let pTargetY = 0;
      const parallaxNodes = document.querySelectorAll('.node, .card-stack');

      document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => { mouseX = e.clientX; mouseY = e.clientY; });

      function animateParallax() {
        pTargetX += ((mouseX - window.innerWidth / 2) / 100 - pTargetX) * 0.1;
        pTargetY += ((mouseY - window.innerHeight / 2) / 100 - pTargetY) * 0.1;
        parallaxNodes.forEach(node => {
          const depth = node.getAttribute('data-depth') || 0.2;
          node.style.transform = `translate(${pTargetX * (depth * 20)}px, ${pTargetY * (depth * 20)}px)`;
        });
        requestAnimationFrame(animateParallax);
      }
      animateParallax();


      // 3. Canvas Tools & Panning Setup
      const viewport = document.getElementById('viewport');
      const workspace = document.getElementById('workspace');
      let currentTool = 'pointer'; let isPanning = false; let panX = 0; let panY = 0; let startX = 0; let startY = 0;

      function setTool(tool) {
        currentTool = tool;
        document.querySelectorAll('.canvas-tools .tool-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
        if (tool !== 'add') document.getElementById(tool + 'Btn').classList.add('active');
        viewport.style.cursor = tool === 'hand' ? 'grab' : (tool === 'text' ? 'text' : (tool === 'folder' || tool === 'tile' ? 'crosshair' : 'default'));
      }

      ['pointer', 'hand', 'text', 'folder', 'tile'].forEach(t => document.getElementById(t + 'Btn').addEventListener('click', () => setTool(t)));

      window.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
        if (document.activeElement.tagName === 'INPUT' || document.activeElement.isContentEditable) return;
        if (e.code === 'Space' && currentTool !== 'hand') { e.preventDefault(); viewport.style.cursor = 'grab'; }
        else if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 'h') setTool('hand');
        else if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') setTool('pointer');
        else if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 't') setTool('text');
        else if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 'f') setTool('folder');
        else if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 'c') setTool('tile');
      });

      window.addEventListener('keyup', (e) => {
        if (e.code === 'Space' && document.activeElement.tagName !== 'INPUT' && currentTool !== 'hand') { setTool(currentTool); isPanning = false; }
      });

      viewport.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
        if (currentTool === 'text' || currentTool === 'folder' || currentTool === 'tile') return;
        const isSpaceHeld = viewport.style.cursor === 'grab' || viewport.style.cursor === 'grabbing';
        if (currentTool !== 'hand' && !isSpaceHeld && e.button !== 1) return;

        // Prevents text and objects from being highlighted while dragging
        e.preventDefault();
        document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';

        isPanning = true; startX = e.clientX - panX; startY = e.clientY - panY; viewport.style.cursor = 'grabbing';
        document.body.classList.add('dragging-state');
      });

      window.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
        if (!isPanning) return;
        panX = e.clientX - startX; panY = e.clientY - startY;
        workspace.style.transform = `translate(calc(-50% + ${panX}px), calc(-50% + ${panY}px))`;
        viewport.style.backgroundPosition = `calc(50% + ${panX}px) calc(50% + ${panY}px)`;
      });

      window.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
        document.body.classList.remove('dragging-state');
        if (isPanning) {
          isPanning = false;
          viewport.style.cursor = currentTool === 'hand' ? 'grab' : 'default';
          // Restores standard text selection when you stop dragging
          document.body.style.userSelect = '';
        }
      });

      // 4. Canvas Creation Logic
      viewport.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        if (e.target.closest('.generic-overlay') || e.target.closest('.canvas-tools') || e.target.closest('.hero-title') ||
          e.target.closest('.hero-cta') || e.target.closest('.vault-pet-wrapper') || e.target.closest('.toast') ||
          e.target.closest('.folder') || e.target.closest('.delete-btn') || e.target.closest('nav')) return;
        if (isPanning) return;

        if (currentTool === 'text' || currentTool === 'folder' || currentTool === 'tile') {
          const rect = workspace.getBoundingClientRect();
          const x = e.clientX - rect.left; const y = e.clientY - rect.top;

          if (currentTool === 'text') createTextNode(x, y);
          if (currentTool === 'folder') createFolderNode(x, y);
          if (currentTool === 'tile') createTileNode(x, y);
          setTool('pointer');
        }
      });

      function createTextNode(x, y) {
        const wrapper = document.createElement('div'); wrapper.className = 'custom-text-wrapper'; wrapper.style.left = `${x}px`; wrapper.style.top = `${y}px`;
        const textEl = document.createElement('div'); textEl.className = 'custom-text'; textEl.contentEditable = true; textEl.innerText = 'New Text';
        const delBtn = document.createElement('button'); delBtn.className = 'delete-btn'; delBtn.innerHTML = '×';
        delBtn.onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); wrapper.remove(); speak("Poof! Gone. 💨"); };
        wrapper.appendChild(textEl); wrapper.appendChild(delBtn); workspace.appendChild(wrapper);
        textEl.focus(); document.execCommand('selectAll', false, null); speak("A new thought! 📝");
      }

      function createFolderNode(x, y) {
        const folderId = 'folder-' + Date.now();
        const fw = document.createElement('div'); fw.className = 'custom-folder'; fw.style.left = `${x}px`; fw.style.top = `${y}px`;
        fw.dataset.folderId = folderId;
        fw.innerHTML = `<button class="delete-btn">×</button><div class="folder mini-folder" onclick="this.classList.toggle('open')"><div class="folder__back"><div class="folder__front"></div></div></div><div class="folder-label" contenteditable="true">New Folder</div>`;

        const select = document.getElementById('folderSelect');
        const option = document.createElement('option');
        option.value = folderId;
        option.text = '📁 New Folder';
        option.dataset.folderId = folderId;
        select.appendChild(option);

        fw.querySelector('.delete-btn').onclick = (e) => {
          e.stopPropagation();
          fw.remove();
          const opt = select.querySelector(`option[data-folder-id="${folderId}"]`);
          if (opt) opt.remove();
          speak("Folder deleted! 🗑️");
        };

        const label = fw.querySelector('.folder-label');
        label.addEventListener('blur', () => {
          const opt = select.querySelector(`option[data-folder-id="${folderId}"]`);
          if (opt) opt.text = '📁 ' + label.innerText;
        });

        workspace.appendChild(fw);
        label.focus();
        document.execCommand('selectAll', false, null);
        speak("Space for new refs! 📁");
      }

      function createTileNode(x, y) {
        const tw = document.createElement('div'); tw.className = 'custom-tile-wrapper'; tw.style.left = `${x}px`; tw.style.top = `${y}px`;
        tw.innerHTML = `<button class="delete-btn">×</button><div class="icard icard-white"><div class="card-illo"><svg viewBox="0 0 52 52" class="illo-stroke"><circle cx="20" cy="22" r="6"/><circle cx="30" cy="22" r="6"/><circle cx="25" cy="32" r="6"/><circle cx="16" cy="34" r="4" stroke-dasharray="2 2"/><circle cx="35" cy="31" r="4" stroke-dasharray="2 2"/></svg></div><div class="card-title" contenteditable="true" spellcheck="false">New Concept</div><div class="card-by" contenteditable="true" spellcheck="false">BY CREATOR</div></div>`;
        tw.querySelector('.delete-btn').onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); tw.remove(); speak("Tile discarded! 🎴"); };
        workspace.appendChild(tw); tw.querySelector('.card-title').focus(); document.execCommand('selectAll', false, null); speak("A fresh tile! 🎴");
      }

      function createDocNode(x, y, url, title = 'Document') {
        const dw = document.createElement('div');
        dw.className = 'doc-node-wrapper';
        dw.style.left = `${x - 160}px`;
        dw.style.top = `${y - 230}px`;

        // Convert to preview link if it's a Google Doc
        let embedUrl = url;
        if (url.includes('docs.google.com/document/d/')) {
          embedUrl = url.replace(/\/edit.*$/, '/preview').replace(/\/view.*$/, '/preview');
        } else if (url.match(/\.(docx|doc|pdf)$/i)) {
          embedUrl = `https://docs.google.com/gview?url=${encodeURIComponent(url)}&embedded=true`;
        }

        dw.innerHTML = `
      <button class="delete-btn">×</button>
      <div class="doc-card">
        <div class="doc-header">
          <div class="doc-title-pill" contenteditable="true" spellcheck="false">${title}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="doc-iframe-container">
          <iframe class="doc-iframe" src="${embedUrl}"></iframe>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
        dw.querySelector('.delete-btn').onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); dw.remove(); speak("Document removed! 📄"); };
        workspace.appendChild(dw);
        speak("Document embedded! 📄");
      }

      // Node Dragging Logic
      let activeDragNode = null;
      let nodeStartX = 0, nodeStartY = 0, mouseStartX = 0, mouseStartY = 0;

      document.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
        // Add dragging state when interacting with card edges/header
        if (e.target.closest('.doc-card')) {
          document.body.classList.add('dragging-state');
        }

        const header = e.target.closest('.doc-header');
        if (header && !e.target.closest('.doc-title-pill')) {
          // Prevent drag conflict if panning tool or space is active
          const isSpaceHeld = viewport.style.cursor === 'grab' || viewport.style.cursor === 'grabbing';
          if (currentTool === 'hand' || isSpaceHeld || e.button === 1) return;

          e.preventDefault(); // Prevents browser text-selection auto-scroll bug
          document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';

          activeDragNode = header.closest('.doc-node-wrapper');
          mouseStartX = e.clientX;
          mouseStartY = e.clientY;
          nodeStartX = parseFloat(activeDragNode.style.left) || 0;
          nodeStartY = parseFloat(activeDragNode.style.top) || 0;
          activeDragNode.style.zIndex = 100;
        }
      });

      document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
        if (activeDragNode) {
          const dx = e.clientX - mouseStartX;
          const dy = e.clientY - mouseStartY;
          activeDragNode.style.left = `${nodeStartX + dx}px`;
          activeDragNode.style.top = `${nodeStartY + dy}px`;
        }
      });

      document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
        if (activeDragNode) {
          activeDragNode.style.zIndex = '';
          activeDragNode = null;
          document.body.style.userSelect = '';
        }
        document.body.classList.remove('dragging-state');
      });

      // 5. Companion Pet Logic
      const petSpeech = document.getElementById('petSpeech');
      const phrases = ["Pixel perfect. 😉", "Your canvas looks infinite!", "Press T to write!", "Press F to organize!", "Press C to drop a tile!", "Flawless composition ✨", "Creative OS online."];

      window.speak = function (customText = null) {
        petSpeech.textContent = customText || phrases[Math.floor(Math.random() * phrases.length)];
        petSpeech.classList.add('show');
        if (window.petSpeechTimer) clearTimeout(window.petSpeechTimer);
        window.petSpeechTimer = setTimeout(() => petSpeech.classList.remove('show'), 3000);
      };

      document.getElementById('petMew').addEventListener('click', () => speak("Mew! I love good UI! ✨"));
      document.getElementById('petGengar').addEventListener('click', () => speak("Gengar! 👻"));
      document.getElementById('petSnorlax').addEventListener('click', () => speak("Snorlax... zzz... 💤"));
      document.getElementById('petGreninja').addEventListener('click', () => speak("Ninja! 🥷"));
      document.getElementById('petPsyduck').addEventListener('click', () => speak("Psy... duck? 🦆"));

      setInterval(() => { if (Math.random() > 0.7 && !petSpeech.classList.contains('show')) speak(); }, 10000);
      setTimeout(() => speak("Hi! We're your Canvas Spirits!"), 1500);

      // Theme Toggle Logic
      const themeToggle = document.getElementById('themeToggle');
      themeToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
        document.body.classList.toggle('dark-theme');
        if (document.body.classList.contains('dark-theme')) {
          themeToggle.textContent = '☀️';
          speak("Dark mode engaged! 🌙");
        } else {
          themeToggle.textContent = '🌙';
          speak("Back to the light! ☀️");
        }
      });

      // 6. Generic Modal Handlers
      document.querySelectorAll('.close-generic').forEach(btn => btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        const overlay = e.target.closest('.generic-overlay');
        overlay.classList.add('hidden');

        // Automatically close the canvas folder when closing the folder modal
        if (overlay.id === 'folderContentModal') {
          document.getElementById('mainFolderBtn').classList.remove('open');
        }
      }));

      // Close overlays when clicking outside the box (except the mandatory login modal)
      document.querySelectorAll('.generic-overlay').forEach(overlay => {
        overlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
          if (e.target === overlay && overlay.id !== 'loginModal') {
            overlay.classList.add('hidden');
            if (overlay.id === 'folderContentModal') {
              document.getElementById('mainFolderBtn').classList.remove('open');
            }
          }
        });
      });

      // Toast Close Handler Fix (Using proper event listener)
      document.getElementById('toastCloseBtn').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        document.getElementById('toast').classList.add('hidden');
      });

      // 7. Modals: Login & Storage
      let isLoggedIn = false;
      const loginModal = document.getElementById('loginModal');
      const storageModal = document.getElementById('storageModal');
      const googleLoginBtn = document.getElementById('googleLoginBtn');
      const vaultTriggers = document.querySelectorAll('.vault-trigger');

      vaultTriggers.forEach(btn => {
        btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
          e.preventDefault();
          if (!isLoggedIn) {
            loginModal.classList.remove('hidden');
            speak("Security check! Identify yourself. 🕵️‍♀️");
          } else {
            storageModal.classList.remove('hidden');
            speak("Checking Vault capacity! ☁️");
          }
        });
      });

      googleLoginBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const originalContent = googleLoginBtn.innerHTML;
        googleLoginBtn.innerHTML = '<span class="auth-loader"></span> Authenticating...';
        googleLoginBtn.style.pointerEvents = 'none';

        setTimeout(() => {
          googleLoginBtn.innerHTML = originalContent;
          googleLoginBtn.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
          loginModal.classList.add('hidden');
          isLoggedIn = true;
          speak("Welcome back, Creator! 🎉");

          const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
          toast.classList.remove('hidden');
          toast.querySelector('.toast-message').innerHTML = `System Auth: <span class="toast-highlight">Vault Unlocked</span>`;

          vaultTriggers.forEach(btn => {
            btn.innerText = "Vault Unlocked 🔓";
            btn.style.background = "var(--blue)";
            btn.style.color = "var(--white)";
          });
        }, 1500);
      });

      // 8. Modals: Boards & Search
      document.getElementById('navBoards').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        document.getElementById('boardsModal').classList.remove('hidden');
        speak("Looking at your collections! 📁");
      });

      document.getElementById('navSearch').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        document.getElementById('searchModal').classList.remove('hidden');
        setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('searchInput').focus(), 100);
        speak("Let's find something! 🔍");
      });

      // 9. Modals: Add Item
      const addModal = document.getElementById('addModal');
      document.getElementById('addBtn').addEventListener('click', () => { addModal.classList.remove('hidden'); speak("What are we saving today? ✨"); });

      const addTypeTabs = addModal.querySelectorAll('.type-tab');
      const addInputSections = addModal.querySelectorAll('.input-section');
      addTypeTabs.forEach(tab => {
        tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
          addTypeTabs.forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active')); tab.classList.add('active');
          addInputSections.forEach(sec => sec.classList.remove('active')); document.getElementById('input-' + tab.dataset.type).classList.add('active');
          const select = document.getElementById('folderSelect');
          if (tab.dataset.type === 'prompt') select.value = 'prompts';
          else if (tab.dataset.type === 'image') select.value = 'images';
          else if (tab.dataset.type === 'design') select.value = 'design';
          else if (tab.dataset.type === 'link') select.value = 'links';
          else if (tab.dataset.type === 'react') select.value = 'react';
          else select.value = 'general';
        });
      });

      const saveItemBtn = document.getElementById('saveItemBtn');
      saveItemBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const originalText = saveItemBtn.innerText;
        saveItemBtn.innerHTML = '<span class="auth-loader" style="border-top-color:white;"></span> Saving...';
        saveItemBtn.style.pointerEvents = 'none';

        setTimeout(() => {
          saveItemBtn.innerText = originalText; saveItemBtn.style.pointerEvents = 'auto'; addModal.classList.add('hidden');
          const activeTab = addModal.querySelector('.type-tab.active').innerText;
          const folder = document.getElementById('folderSelect').options[document.getElementById('folderSelect').selectedIndex].text;

          const toast = document.getElementById('toast'); toast.classList.remove('hidden');
          toast.querySelector('.toast-message').innerHTML = `Saved ${activeTab} to <span class="toast-highlight">${folder}</span>`;
          speak(`Stored safely in ${folder}! 📂`);

          // Add Docs to Canvas
          const activeTabType = addModal.querySelector('.type-tab.active').dataset.type;
          if (activeTabType === 'docs') {
            const docInput = document.querySelector('#input-docs input[type="url"]');
            if (docInput && docInput.value) {
              const rect = workspace.getBoundingClientRect();
              const centerX = (window.innerWidth / 2) - rect.left;
              const centerY = (window.innerHeight / 2) - rect.top;
              createDocNode(centerX, centerY, docInput.value, 'New Document');
              docInput.value = ''; // clear input
            }
          }
        }, 800);
      });

      // 10. Folder Content Modal
      const folderContentModal = document.getElementById('folderContentModal');
      const mainFolderBtn = document.getElementById('mainFolderBtn');

      mainFolderBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        mainFolderBtn.classList.add('open');
        setTimeout(() => {
          folderContentModal.classList.remove('hidden');
          speak("Opening the main directory! 📂");
        }, 300);
      });

      const folderTabs = folderContentModal.querySelectorAll('.dock-item');
      const folderSections = folderContentModal.querySelectorAll('.content-section');

      folderTabs.forEach(tab => {
        tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
          folderTabs.forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active')); tab.classList.add('active');
          folderSections.forEach(sec => sec.classList.remove('active')); document.getElementById('content-' + tab.dataset.content).classList.add('active');
        });
      });

      // 11. Image Viewer & Copy Functionality
      const fullscreenModal = document.getElementById('fullscreenModal');
      const fullscreenImg = document.getElementById('fullscreenImg');

      window.openFullscreen = function (src) {
        fullscreenImg.src = src;
        fullscreenModal.classList.remove('hidden');
        speak("Taking a closer look! 🔍");
      };

      document.getElementById('closeFullscreenBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
        fullscreenModal.classList.add('hidden');
      });

      fullscreenModal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        if (e.target === fullscreenModal) fullscreenModal.classList.add('hidden');
      });

      window.copyPrompt = function (text) {
        // Hidden textarea fallback for iframes (ensures smooth copying)
        const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
        textarea.value = text;
        document.body.appendChild(textarea);
        textarea.select();
        try {
          document.execCommand('copy');
          const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
          toast.classList.remove('hidden');
          toast.querySelector('.toast-message').innerHTML = `Prompt <span class="toast-highlight">Copied</span> to clipboard!`;
          speak("Copied to clipboard! 📋");
        } catch (err) {
          console.error('Failed to copy', err);
        }
        document.body.removeChild(textarea);
      };

      window.toggleHeart = function (btn, event) {
        event.stopPropagation();
        btn.classList.toggle('active');
        const isFilled = btn.classList.contains('active');
        if (isFilled) {
          speak('Added to favorites! ❤️');
        } else {
          speak('Removed from favorites');
        }
      };

      window.downloadItem = function (event) {
        event.stopPropagation();
        speak('Downloading item! 📥');
      };

      window.copyCardContent = function (btn, event) {
        event.stopPropagation();
        const card = btn.closest('.grid-card');
        if (card && card.hasAttribute('onclick')) {
          const clickStr = card.getAttribute('onclick');
          if (clickStr.includes('copyPrompt')) {
            card.click();
          } else {
            const title = card.querySelector('.grid-card-title').innerText;
            if (title.includes('Stripe')) {
              window.copyPrompt('https://stripe.com');
            } else {
              window.copyPrompt(title);
            }
          }
        }
      };

    });
  </script>

</body>

</html>

    .tool-btn {
      width: 44px;
      height: 44px;
      border-radius: 10px;
      border: none;
      background: transparent;
      cursor: pointer;
      font-size: 20px;
      display: flex;
      align-items: center;
      justify-content: center;
      transition: all 0.2s;
      color: var(--text);
      position: relative;
    }

    .tool-btn:hover {
      background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05);
    }

    .tool-btn.active {
      background: var(--blue);
      color: var(--white);
      box-shadow: 0 4px 12px rgba(45, 91, 227, 0.3);
    }

    .tool-btn.primary-add {
      background: var(--blue);
      color: var(--white);
      border-radius: 50%;
      margin-top: 8px;
      font-size: 24px;
      font-weight: 300;
      box-shadow: 0 4px 14px rgba(45, 91, 227, 0.3);
    }

    .tool-btn.primary-add:hover {
      background: var(--blue-hover);
      transform: scale(1.05);
      box-shadow: 0 8px 20px rgba(45, 91, 227, 0.4);
    }

    .tool-divider {
      height: 1px;
      width: 100%;
      background: var(--border);
      margin: 4px 0;
    }

    /* ── DYNAMIC CANVAS ELEMENTS ── */
    .custom-text-wrapper {
      position: absolute;
      transform: translate(-50%, -50%);
      z-index: 50;
    }

    .custom-text {
      font-family: 'Google Sans Display', sans-serif;
      font-size: 32px;

  <!-- ── INTERACTIVE SCRIPTS ── -->
  <script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {

      // 1. Magnetic Buttons
      const magnets = document.querySelectorAll('.magnetic');
      magnets.forEach(magnet => {
        magnet.addEventListener('mousemove', function (e) {
          const rect = this.getBoundingClientRect();
          const x = e.clientX - rect.left - rect.width / 2;
          const y = e.clientY - rect.top - rect.height / 2;
          const strength = this.getAttribute('data-strength') || 20;
          this.style.transform = `translate(${(x / rect.width) * strength}px, ${(y / rect.height) * strength}px) scale(1.05) rotate(${(x / rect.width) * strength * 0.1}deg)`;
        });
        magnet.addEventListener('mouseleave', function () { this.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px) scale(1) rotate(0deg)'; });
      });

      // 2. Parallax Effects
      let mouseX = window.innerWidth / 2; let mouseY = window.innerHeight / 2;
      let pTargetX = 0; let pTargetY = 0;
      const parallaxNodes = document.querySelectorAll('.node, .card-stack');

      document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => { mouseX = e.clientX; mouseY = e.clientY; });

      function animateParallax() {
        pTargetX += ((mouseX - window.innerWidth / 2) / 100 - pTargetX) * 0.1;
        pTargetY += ((mouseY - window.innerHeight / 2) / 100 - pTargetY) * 0.1;
        parallaxNodes.forEach(node => {
          const depth = node.getAttribute('data-depth') || 0.2;
          node.style.transform = `translate(${pTargetX * (depth * 20)}px, ${pTargetY * (depth * 20)}px)`;
        });
        requestAnimationFrame(animateParallax);
      }
      animateParallax();


      // 3. Canvas Tools & Panning Setup
      const viewport = document.getElementById('viewport');
      const workspace = document.getElementById('workspace');
      let currentTool = 'pointer'; let isPanning = false; let panX = 0; let panY = 0; let startX = 0; let startY = 0;

      function setTool(tool) {
        currentTool = tool;
        document.querySelectorAll('.canvas-tools .tool-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
        if (tool !== 'add') document.getElementById(tool + 'Btn').classList.add('active');
        viewport.style.cursor = tool === 'hand' ? 'grab' : (tool === 'text' ? 'text' : (tool === 'folder' || tool === 'tile' ? 'crosshair' : 'default'));
      }

      ['pointer', 'hand', 'text', 'folder', 'tile'].forEach(t => document.getElementById(t + 'Btn').addEventListener('click', () => setTool(t)));

      window.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
        if (document.activeElement.tagName === 'INPUT' || document.activeElement.isContentEditable || document.activeElement.tagName === 'TEXTAREA') return;
        if (e.code === 'Space' && currentTool !== 'hand') { e.preventDefault(); viewport.style.cursor = 'grab'; }
        else if (e.key === '/') {
          e.preventDefault();
          document.getElementById('searchModal').classList.remove('hidden');
          setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('searchInput').focus(), 100);
          speak("Let's find something! 🔍");
        }
        else if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 'h') setTool('hand');
        else if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 'v') setTool('pointer');
        else if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 't') setTool('text');
        else if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 'f') setTool('folder');
        else if (e.key.toLowerCase() === 'c') setTool('tile');
      });

      window.addEventListener('keyup', (e) => {
        if (e.code === 'Space' && document.activeElement.tagName !== 'INPUT' && currentTool !== 'hand') { setTool(currentTool); isPanning = false; }
      });

      viewport.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
        if (currentTool === 'text' || currentTool === 'folder' || currentTool === 'tile') return;
        const isSpaceHeld = viewport.style.cursor === 'grab' || viewport.style.cursor === 'grabbing';
        if (currentTool !== 'hand' && !isSpaceHeld && e.button !== 1) return;

        // Prevents text and objects from being highlighted while dragging
        e.preventDefault();
        document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';

        isPanning = true; startX = e.clientX - panX; startY = e.clientY - panY; viewport.style.cursor = 'grabbing';
        document.body.classList.add('dragging-state');
      });

      window.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
        if (!isPanning) return;
        panX = e.clientX - startX; panY = e.clientY - startY;
        workspace.style.transform = `translate(calc(-50% + ${panX}px), calc(-50% + ${panY}px))`;
        viewport.style.backgroundPosition = `calc(50% + ${panX}px) calc(50% + ${panY}px)`;
      });

      window.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
        document.body.classList.remove('dragging-state');
        if (isPanning) {
          isPanning = false;
          viewport.style.cursor = currentTool === 'hand' ? 'grab' : 'default';
          // Restores standard text selection when you stop dragging
          document.body.style.userSelect = '';
        }
      });

      // 4. Canvas Creation Logic
      viewport.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        if (e.target.closest('.generic-overlay') || e.target.closest('.canvas-tools') || e.target.closest('.hero-title') ||
          e.target.closest('.hero-cta') || e.target.closest('.vault-pet-wrapper') || e.target.closest('.toast') ||
          e.target.closest('.folder') || e.target.closest('.delete-btn') || e.target.closest('nav')) return;
        if (isPanning) return;

        if (currentTool === 'text' || currentTool === 'folder' || currentTool === 'tile') {
          const rect = workspace.getBoundingClientRect();
          const x = e.clientX - rect.left; const y = e.clientY - rect.top;

          if (currentTool === 'text') createTextNode(x, y);
          if (currentTool === 'folder') createFolderNode(x, y);
          if (currentTool === 'tile') createTileNode(x, y);
          setTool('pointer');
        }
      });

      function createTextNode(x, y) {
        const wrapper = document.createElement('div'); wrapper.className = 'custom-text-wrapper'; wrapper.style.left = `${x}px`; wrapper.style.top = `${y}px`;
        const textEl = document.createElement('div'); textEl.className = 'custom-text'; textEl.contentEditable = true; textEl.innerText = 'New Text';
        const delBtn = document.createElement('button'); delBtn.className = 'delete-btn'; delBtn.innerHTML = '×';
        delBtn.onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); wrapper.remove(); speak("Poof! Gone. 💨"); };
        wrapper.appendChild(textEl); wrapper.appendChild(delBtn); workspace.appendChild(wrapper);
        textEl.focus(); document.execCommand('selectAll', false, null); speak("A new thought! 📝");
      }

      // ── Custom folder registry: folderId → [{label, icon, value}]
      const folderRegistry = new Map();

      function createFolderNode(x, y) {
        const folderId = 'folder-' + Date.now();
        folderRegistry.set(folderId, []);

        const fw = document.createElement('div'); fw.className = 'custom-folder'; fw.style.left = `${x}px`; fw.style.top = `${y}px`;
        fw.dataset.folderId = folderId;
        fw.innerHTML = `<button class="delete-btn">×</button><div class="folder mini-folder"><div class="folder__back"><div class="folder__front"></div></div></div><div class="folder-label" contenteditable="true">New Folder</div>`;

        const select = document.getElementById('folderSelect');
        const option = document.createElement('option');
        option.value = folderId;
        option.text = '📁 New Folder';
        option.dataset.folderId = folderId;
        select.appendChild(option);

        // Open peek popup on folder click (but not delete or label)
        fw.querySelector('.folder').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
          e.stopPropagation();
          const labelText = fw.querySelector('.folder-label').innerText.trim() || 'New Folder';
          openFolderPeek(folderId, labelText);
        });

        fw.querySelector('.delete-btn').onclick = (e) => {
          e.stopPropagation();
          fw.remove();
          folderRegistry.delete(folderId);
          const opt = select.querySelector(`option[data-folder-id="${folderId}"]`);
          if (opt) opt.remove();
          speak("Folder deleted! 🗑️");
        };

        const label = fw.querySelector('.folder-label');
        label.addEventListener('blur', () => {
          const opt = select.querySelector(`option[data-folder-id="${folderId}"]`);
          if (opt) opt.text = '📁 ' + label.innerText;
        });

        workspace.appendChild(fw);
        label.focus();
        document.execCommand('selectAll', false, null);
        speak("Space for new refs! 📁");
      }

      function openFolderPeek(folderId, folderName) {
        const overlay = document.getElementById('folderPeekOverlay');
        document.getElementById('folderPeekTitle').textContent = '📁 ' + folderName;
        overlay.dataset.activeFolderId = folderId;
        renderFolderPeek(folderId);
        overlay.classList.remove('hidden');
        speak(`Peeking into ${folderName}! 📂`);
      }

      function renderFolderPeek(folderId) {
        const list = document.getElementById('folderPeekList');
        const empty = document.getElementById('folderPeekEmpty');
        const items = folderRegistry.get(folderId) || [];
        list.innerHTML = '';
        if (items.length === 0) {
          empty.style.display = 'block';
        } else {
          empty.style.display = 'none';
          items.forEach((item, idx) => {
            const row = document.createElement('div');
            row.style.cssText = 'display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;padding:10px 14px;border-radius:12px;background:var(--glass-bg);border:1px solid var(--border);';
            row.innerHTML = `
              <span style="font-size:22px;flex-shrink:0">${item.icon}</span>
              <div style="flex:1;min-width:0">
                <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${item.label}</div>
                <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--muted);margin-top:2px;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${item.value || '—'}</div>
              </div>
              <button title="Remove" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;color:var(--muted);font-size:16px;flex-shrink:0;" data-idx="${idx}">×</button>
            `;
            row.querySelector('button').addEventListener('click', () => {
              items.splice(idx, 1);
              renderFolderPeek(folderId);
            });
            list.appendChild(row);
          });
        }
      }

      document.getElementById('closeFolderPeek').addEventListener('click', () => {
        document.getElementById('folderPeekOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
      });
      document.getElementById('folderPeekOverlay').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        if (e.target === document.getElementById('folderPeekOverlay'))
          document.getElementById('folderPeekOverlay').classList.add('hidden');
      });

      function createTileNode(x, y) {
        const tw = document.createElement('div'); tw.className = 'custom-tile-wrapper'; tw.style.left = `${x}px`; tw.style.top = `${y}px`;
        tw.innerHTML = `<button class="delete-btn">×</button><div class="icard icard-white"><div class="card-illo"><svg viewBox="0 0 52 52" class="illo-stroke"><circle cx="20" cy="22" r="6"/><circle cx="30" cy="22" r="6"/><circle cx="25" cy="32" r="6"/><circle cx="16" cy="34" r="4" stroke-dasharray="2 2"/><circle cx="35" cy="31" r="4" stroke-dasharray="2 2"/></svg></div><div class="card-title" contenteditable="true" spellcheck="false">New Concept</div><div class="card-by" contenteditable="true" spellcheck="false">BY CREATOR</div></div>`;
        tw.querySelector('.delete-btn').onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); tw.remove(); speak("Tile discarded! 🎴"); };
        workspace.appendChild(tw); tw.querySelector('.card-title').focus(); document.execCommand('selectAll', false, null); speak("A fresh tile! 🎴");
      }

      function createDocNode(x, y, url, title = 'Document') {
        const dw = document.createElement('div');
        dw.className = 'doc-node-wrapper';
        // Account for canvas pan offset so node appears near viewport center
        dw.style.left = `${x - 160}px`;
        dw.style.top = `${y - 120}px`;

        // Convert to preview link if it's a Google Doc
        let embedUrl = url;
        if (url.includes('docs.google.com/document/d/')) {
          embedUrl = url.replace(/\/edit.*$/, '/preview').replace(/\/view.*$/, '/preview');
        } else if (url.match(/\.(docx|doc|pdf)$/i)) {
          embedUrl = `https://docs.google.com/gview?url=${encodeURIComponent(url)}&embedded=true`;
        }

        dw.innerHTML = `
      <button class="delete-btn">×</button>
      <div class="doc-card">
        <div class="doc-header">
          <div class="doc-title-pill" contenteditable="true" spellcheck="false">${title}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="doc-iframe-container">
          <iframe class="doc-iframe" src="${embedUrl}"></iframe>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
        dw.querySelector('.delete-btn').onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); dw.remove(); speak("Document removed! 📄"); };
        workspace.appendChild(dw);
        speak("Document embedded! 📄");
      }

      // Node Dragging Logic
      let activeDragNode = null;
      let nodeStartX = 0, nodeStartY = 0, mouseStartX = 0, mouseStartY = 0;

      document.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
        // Add dragging state when interacting with card edges/header
        if (e.target.closest('.doc-card')) {
          document.body.classList.add('dragging-state');
        }

        const header = e.target.closest('.doc-header');
        if (header && !e.target.closest('.doc-title-pill')) {
          // Prevent drag conflict if panning tool or space is active
          const isSpaceHeld = viewport.style.cursor === 'grab' || viewport.style.cursor === 'grabbing';
          if (currentTool === 'hand' || isSpaceHeld || e.button === 1) return;

          e.preventDefault(); // Prevents browser text-selection auto-scroll bug
          document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';

          activeDragNode = header.closest('.doc-node-wrapper');
          mouseStartX = e.clientX;
          mouseStartY = e.clientY;
          nodeStartX = parseFloat(activeDragNode.style.left) || 0;
          nodeStartY = parseFloat(activeDragNode.style.top) || 0;
          activeDragNode.style.zIndex = 100;
        }
      });

      document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
        if (activeDragNode) {
          const dx = e.clientX - mouseStartX;
          const dy = e.clientY - mouseStartY;
          activeDragNode.style.left = `${nodeStartX + dx}px`;
          activeDragNode.style.top = `${nodeStartY + dy}px`;
        }
      });

      document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
        if (activeDragNode) {
          activeDragNode.style.zIndex = '';
          activeDragNode = null;
          document.body.style.userSelect = '';
        }
        document.body.classList.remove('dragging-state');
      });

      // 5. Companion Pet Logic
      const petSpeech = document.getElementById('petSpeech');
      const phrases = ["Pixel perfect. 😉", "Your canvas looks infinite!", "Press T to write!", "Press F to organize!", "Press C to drop a tile!", "Flawless composition ✨", "Creative OS online."];

      window.speak = function (customText = null) {
        petSpeech.textContent = customText || phrases[Math.floor(Math.random() * phrases.length)];
        petSpeech.classList.add('show');
        if (window.petSpeechTimer) clearTimeout(window.petSpeechTimer);
        window.petSpeechTimer = setTimeout(() => petSpeech.classList.remove('show'), 3000);
      };

      document.getElementById('petMew').addEventListener('click', () => speak("Mew! I love good UI! ✨"));
      document.getElementById('petGengar').addEventListener('click', () => speak("Gengar! 👻"));
      document.getElementById('petSnorlax').addEventListener('click', () => speak("Snorlax... zzz... 💤"));
      document.getElementById('petGreninja').addEventListener('click', () => speak("Ninja! 🥷"));
      document.getElementById('petPsyduck').addEventListener('click', () => speak("Psy... duck? 🦆"));

      setInterval(() => { if (Math.random() > 0.7 && !petSpeech.classList.contains('show')) speak(); }, 10000);
      setTimeout(() => speak("Hi! We're your Canvas Spirits!"), 1500);

      // Theme Toggle Logic
      const themeToggle = document.getElementById('themeToggle');
      themeToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
        document.body.classList.toggle('dark-theme');
        if (document.body.classList.contains('dark-theme')) {
          themeToggle.textContent = '☀️';
          speak("Dark mode engaged! 🌙");
        } else {
          themeToggle.textContent = '🌙';
          speak("Back to the light! ☀️");
        }
      });

      // 6. Generic Modal Handlers
      document.querySelectorAll('.close-generic').forEach(btn => btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        const overlay = e.target.closest('.generic-overlay');
        overlay.classList.add('hidden');

        // Automatically close the canvas folder when closing the folder modal
        if (overlay.id === 'folderContentModal') {
          document.getElementById('mainFolderBtn').classList.remove('open');
        }
      }));

      // Close overlays when clicking outside the box (except the mandatory login modal)
      document.querySelectorAll('.generic-overlay').forEach(overlay => {
        overlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
          if (e.target === overlay && overlay.id !== 'loginModal') {
            overlay.classList.add('hidden');
            if (overlay.id === 'folderContentModal') {
              document.getElementById('mainFolderBtn').classList.remove('open');
            }
          }
        });
      });

      // Toast Close Handler Fix (Using proper event listener)
      document.getElementById('toastCloseBtn').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        document.getElementById('toast').classList.add('hidden');
      });

      // 7. Modals: Login & Storage
      let isLoggedIn = false;
      const loginModal = document.getElementById('loginModal');
      const storageModal = document.getElementById('storageModal');
      const googleLoginBtn = document.getElementById('googleLoginBtn');
      const vaultTriggers = document.querySelectorAll('.vault-trigger');

      vaultTriggers.forEach(btn => {
        btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
          e.preventDefault();
          if (!isLoggedIn) {
            loginModal.classList.remove('hidden');
            speak("Security check! Identify yourself. 🕵️‍♀️");
          } else {
            storageModal.classList.remove('hidden');
            speak("Checking Vault capacity! ☁️");
          }
        });
      });

      googleLoginBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const originalContent = googleLoginBtn.innerHTML;
        googleLoginBtn.innerHTML = '<span class="auth-loader"></span> Authenticating...';
        googleLoginBtn.style.pointerEvents = 'none';

        setTimeout(() => {
          googleLoginBtn.innerHTML = originalContent;
          googleLoginBtn.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
          loginModal.classList.add('hidden');
          isLoggedIn = true;
          speak("Welcome back, Creator! 🎉");

          const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
          toast.classList.remove('hidden');
          toast.querySelector('.toast-message').innerHTML = `System Auth: <span class="toast-highlight">Vault Unlocked</span>`;

          vaultTriggers.forEach(btn => {
            btn.innerText = "Vault Unlocked 🔓";
            btn.style.background = "var(--blue)";
            btn.style.color = "var(--white)";
          });
        }, 1500);
      });

      // 8. Modals: Boards & Search
      document.getElementById('navBoards').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        document.getElementById('boardsModal').classList.remove('hidden');
        speak("Looking at your collections! 📁");
      });

      document.getElementById('navSearch').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        document.getElementById('searchModal').classList.remove('hidden');
        setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('searchInput').focus(), 100);
        speak("Let's find something! 🔍");
      });

      // Search filtering: collect all grid-card titles as searchable items
      const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
      const searchResults = document.getElementById('searchResults');
      const searchResultsLabel = document.getElementById('searchResultsLabel');
      const recentSearchChips = document.getElementById('recentSearchChips');

      searchInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
        const q = searchInput.value.trim().toLowerCase();
        searchResults.innerHTML = '';
        if (!q) {
          searchResultsLabel.textContent = 'Recent Searches';
          recentSearchChips.style.display = 'flex';
          return;
        }
        searchResultsLabel.textContent = 'Results';
        recentSearchChips.style.display = 'none';
        // Gather all grid-card titles from the vault directory
        const allCards = document.querySelectorAll('#folderContentModal .grid-card');
        let count = 0;
        allCards.forEach(card => {
          const titleEl = card.querySelector('.grid-card-title');
          if (!titleEl) return;
          const title = titleEl.textContent.trim();
          if (title.toLowerCase().includes(q)) {
            const row = document.createElement('div');
            row.style.cssText = 'display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;padding:10px 12px;border-radius:10px;background:var(--glass-bg);border:1px solid var(--border);cursor:pointer;';
            row.innerHTML = `<span style="font-size:18px">📄</span><span style="font-size:13px;font-weight:500;">${title}</span>`;
            row.onclick = () => { speak(`Found: ${title}! 🔍`); document.getElementById('searchModal').classList.add('hidden'); };
            searchResults.appendChild(row);
            count++;
          }
        });
        if (count === 0) {
          searchResults.innerHTML = '<div style="color:var(--muted);font-size:13px;padding:8px 0;">No matches found</div>';
        }
      });

      // 9. Modals: Add Item
      const addModal = document.getElementById('addModal');

      // Clipboard paste detection: auto-fill the active input when the modal opens
      document.getElementById('addBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
        addModal.classList.remove('hidden');
        speak("What are we saving today? ✨");
        // Try to read clipboard and pre-fill
        try {
          const text = await navigator.clipboard.readText();
          if (!text) return;
          const activeSection = addModal.querySelector('.input-section.active');
          if (!activeSection) return;
          const textarea = activeSection.querySelector('textarea');
          const urlInput = activeSection.querySelector('input[type="url"]');
          const textInput = activeSection.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
          if (textarea && !textarea.value) { textarea.value = text; speak("Pasted from clipboard! 📋"); }
          else if (urlInput && !urlInput.value && (text.startsWith('http://') || text.startsWith('https://'))) { urlInput.value = text; speak("URL detected from clipboard! 🔗"); }
          else if (textInput && !textInput.value) { textInput.value = text; speak("Pasted from clipboard! 📋"); }
        } catch (_) { /* clipboard access denied — silent */ }
      });

      // Also detect paste events globally when the modal is open
      addModal.addEventListener('paste', async (e) => {
        const text = e.clipboardData?.getData('text') || '';
        if (!text) return;
        const activeSection = addModal.querySelector('.input-section.active');
        if (!activeSection) return;
        // Only auto-route if nothing is currently focused inside
        if (activeSection.contains(document.activeElement)) return;
        e.preventDefault();
        const textarea = activeSection.querySelector('textarea');
        const urlInput = activeSection.querySelector('input[type="url"]');
        const textInput = activeSection.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
        if (textarea) { textarea.value = text; textarea.focus(); speak("Pasted! 📋"); }
        else if (urlInput) { urlInput.value = text; urlInput.focus(); speak("Pasted! 📋"); }
        else if (textInput) { textInput.value = text; textInput.focus(); speak("Pasted! 📋"); }
      });

      const addTypeTabs = addModal.querySelectorAll('.type-tab');
      const addInputSections = addModal.querySelectorAll('.input-section');
      addTypeTabs.forEach(tab => {
        tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
          addTypeTabs.forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active')); tab.classList.add('active');
          addInputSections.forEach(sec => sec.classList.remove('active')); document.getElementById('input-' + tab.dataset.type).classList.add('active');
          const select = document.getElementById('folderSelect');
          if (tab.dataset.type === 'prompt') select.value = 'prompts';
          else if (tab.dataset.type === 'image') select.value = 'images';
          else if (tab.dataset.type === 'design') select.value = 'design';
          else if (tab.dataset.type === 'link') select.value = 'links';
          else if (tab.dataset.type === 'react') select.value = 'react';
          else select.value = 'general';
        });
      });

      const saveItemBtn = document.getElementById('saveItemBtn');
      saveItemBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const originalText = saveItemBtn.innerText;
        saveItemBtn.innerHTML = '<span class="auth-loader" style="border-top-color:white;"></span> Saving...';
        saveItemBtn.style.pointerEvents = 'none';

        setTimeout(() => {
          saveItemBtn.innerText = originalText; saveItemBtn.style.pointerEvents = 'auto'; addModal.classList.add('hidden');
          const activeTab = addModal.querySelector('.type-tab.active').innerText;
          const folderSel = document.getElementById('folderSelect');
          const folderVal = folderSel.value;
          const folder = folderSel.options[folderSel.selectedIndex].text;

          const toast = document.getElementById('toast'); toast.classList.remove('hidden');
          toast.querySelector('.toast-message').innerHTML = `Saved ${activeTab} to <span class="toast-highlight">${folder}</span>`;
          speak(`Stored safely in ${folder}! 📂`);

          // ── Store in custom folder registry if it's a canvas folder ──
          if (folderRegistry.has(folderVal)) {
            const activeSection = addModal.querySelector('.input-section.active');
            let val = '';
            if (activeSection) {
              const ta = activeSection.querySelector('textarea');
              const url = activeSection.querySelector('input[type="url"]');
              const txt = activeSection.querySelector('input[type="text"]');
              val = (ta?.value || url?.value || txt?.value || '').trim();
            }
            const iconMap = { Prompt:'💬', Link:'🔗', Image:'🖼️', Design:'✦', React:'⚛️', Docs:'📄', PDF:'📑', MD:'📝', Skills:'🧠', ZIP:'🗜️' };
            const icon = iconMap[activeTab] || '📁';
            folderRegistry.get(folderVal).push({ label: activeTab, icon, value: val });
          }

          // Add Docs to Canvas
          const activeTabType = addModal.querySelector('.type-tab.active').dataset.type;
          if (activeTabType === 'docs') {
            const docInput = document.querySelector('#input-docs input[type="url"]');
            if (docInput && docInput.value) {
              const rect = workspace.getBoundingClientRect();
              const centerX = (window.innerWidth / 2) - rect.left;
              const centerY = (window.innerHeight / 2) - rect.top;
              createDocNode(centerX, centerY, docInput.value, 'New Document');
              docInput.value = '';
            }
          }
        }, 800);
      });

      // 10. Folder Content Modal
      const folderContentModal = document.getElementById('folderContentModal');
      const mainFolderBtn = document.getElementById('mainFolderBtn');

      mainFolderBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        mainFolderBtn.classList.add('open');
        setTimeout(() => {
          folderContentModal.classList.remove('hidden');
          speak("Opening the main directory! 📂");
        }, 300);
      });

      const folderTabs = folderContentModal.querySelectorAll('.dock-item');
      const folderSections = folderContentModal.querySelectorAll('.content-section');

      folderTabs.forEach(tab => {
        tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
          folderTabs.forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active')); tab.classList.add('active');
          folderSections.forEach(sec => sec.classList.remove('active')); document.getElementById('content-' + tab.dataset.content).classList.add('active');
        });
      });

      // 11. Image Viewer & Copy Functionality
      const fullscreenModal = document.getElementById('fullscreenModal');
      const fullscreenImg = document.getElementById('fullscreenImg');

      window.openFullscreen = function (src) {
        fullscreenImg.src = src;
        fullscreenModal.classList.remove('hidden');
        speak("Taking a closer look! 🔍");
      };

      document.getElementById('closeFullscreenBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
        fullscreenModal.classList.add('hidden');
      });

      fullscreenModal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        if (e.target === fullscreenModal) fullscreenModal.classList.add('hidden');
      });

      window.copyPrompt = function (text) {
        // Hidden textarea fallback for iframes (ensures smooth copying)
        const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
        textarea.value = text;
        document.body.appendChild(textarea);
        textarea.select();
        try {
          document.execCommand('copy');
          const toast = document.getElementById('toast');
          toast.classList.remove('hidden');
          toast.querySelector('.toast-message').innerHTML = `Prompt <span class="toast-highlight">Copied</span> to clipboard!`;
          speak("Copied to clipboard! 📋");
        } catch (err) {
          console.error('Failed to copy', err);
        }
        document.body.removeChild(textarea);
      };

      window.toggleHeart = function (btn, event) {
        event.stopPropagation();
        btn.classList.toggle('active');
        const isFilled = btn.classList.contains('active');
        if (isFilled) {
          speak('Added to favorites! ❤️');
        } else {
          speak('Removed from favorites');
        }
      };

      window.downloadItem = function (event) {
        event.stopPropagation();
        speak('Downloading item! 📥');
      };

      window.copyCardContent = function (btn, event) {
        event.stopPropagation();
        const card = btn.closest('.grid-card');
        if (card && card.hasAttribute('onclick')) {
          const clickStr = card.getAttribute('onclick');
          if (clickStr.includes('copyPrompt')) {
            card.click();
          } else {
            const title = card.querySelector('.grid-card-title').innerText;
            if (title.includes('Stripe')) {
              window.copyPrompt('https://stripe.com');
            } else {
              window.copyPrompt(title);
            }
          }
        }
      };

      // Wire drag-and-drop feedback for all drop zones (click does NOT open file picker)
      document.querySelectorAll('.drop-zone').forEach(zone => {
        zone.addEventListener('click', e => e.preventDefault()); // block file-picker on click

        zone.addEventListener('dragover', e => {
          e.preventDefault();
          zone.classList.add('drag-over');
        });
        zone.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
          zone.classList.remove('drag-over');
        });
        zone.addEventListener('drop', e => {
          e.preventDefault();
          zone.classList.remove('drag-over');
          const files = e.dataTransfer.files;
          if (files.length > 0) {
            zone.innerHTML = `<span style="font-size:24px;display:block;margin-bottom:8px">✅</span><strong>${files[0].name}</strong> ready`;
            speak(`${files[0].name} dropped! 📂`);
          }
        });
      });

    });
  </script>

</body>

</html>
